<script>

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════

// MUSIC — SUSPENSEFUL CINEMATIC

// No melody, no beat at first.

// Dark drone → slow heartbeat pulse → rising

// tension → sudden impact stab → eerie calm

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════

let AC = null, MG = null, muted = false, played = false;


function initCtx() {

if (AC) return;

AC = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();

MG = AC.createGain();

MG.gain.value = 0.18;

MG.connect(AC.destination);

}


function muteToggle() {

muted = !muted;

if (MG) MG.gain.value = muted ? 0 : 0.18;

const el = document.getElementById(‘snd’);

el.textContent = muted ? ‘SOUND OFF’ : ‘SOUND ON’;

el.classList.toggle(‘on’, !muted);

}


// ── filtered sine drone ──

function drone(freq, t, dur, vol, cutoff) {

if (!AC || muted) return;

const o = AC.createOscillator();

const g = AC.createGain();

const lp = AC.createBiquadFilter();

lp.type = ‘lowpass’; lp.frequency.value = cutoff || 400;

o.type = ‘sine’; o.frequency.value = freq;

o.connect(lp); lp.connect(g); g.connect(MG);

g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);

g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol || 0.12, t + 1.2);

g.gain.setValueAtTime(vol || 0.12, t + dur - 1.0);

g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + dur);

o.start(t); o.stop(t + dur + 0.1);

}


// ── noise texture (low rumble / air) ──

function rumble(t, dur, cutoff, vol) {

if (!AC || muted) return;

const sr = AC.sampleRate;

const buf = AC.createBuffer(1, sr * dur, sr);

const d = buf.getChannelData(0);

for (let i = 0; i < d.length; i++) d[i] = Math.random() * 2 - 1;

const src = AC.createBufferSource();

const lp = AC.createBiquadFilter();

const g = AC.createGain();

lp.type = ‘lowpass’; lp.frequency.value = cutoff || 120;

src.buffer = buf;

src.connect(lp); lp.connect(g); g.connect(MG);

g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);

g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol || 0.06, t + dur * 0.2);

g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + dur);

src.start(t); src.stop(t + dur + 0.05);

}


// ── slow heartbeat thud ──

function thud(t, vol) {

if (!AC || muted) return;

const o = AC.createOscillator(), g = AC.createGain();

o.type = ‘sine’;

o.frequency.setValueAtTime(55, t);

o.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(28, t + 0.35);

g.gain.setValueAtTime(vol || 0.45, t);

g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.5);

o.connect(g); g.connect(MG);

o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.55);

// soft second beat (like a heartbeat double-thud)

const o2 = AC.createOscillator(), g2 = AC.createGain();

o2.type = ‘sine’;

o2.frequency.setValueAtTime(50, t + 0.22);

o2.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(25, t + 0.50);

g2.gain.setValueAtTime((vol || 0.45) * 0.55, t + 0.22);

g2.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.55);

o2.connect(g2); g2.connect(MG);

o2.start(t + 0.22); o2.stop(t + 0.6);

}


// ── tension string swell (ascending sine cluster) ──

function swell(rootFreq, t, dur, vol) {

if (!AC || muted) return;

[1, 1.19, 1.498, 1.782].forEach((ratio, i) => {

const o = AC.createOscillator();

const g = AC.createGain();

const lp = AC.createBiquadFilter();

lp.type = ‘lowpass’; lp.frequency.value = 1200;

o.type = ‘sine’;

o.frequency.setValueAtTime(rootFreq * ratio, t);

// very slow vibrato

const lfo = AC.createOscillator();

const lfog = AC.createGain();

lfo.frequency.value = 4.5 + i * 0.3;

lfog.gain.value = 2;

lfo.connect(lfog); lfog.connect(o.frequency);

lfo.start(t); lfo.stop(t + dur + 0.1);

o.connect(lp); lp.connect(g); g.connect(MG);

const v = (vol || 0.06) * (1 - i * 0.18);

g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);

g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(v, t + dur * 0.5);

g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, t + dur);

o.start(t); o.stop(t + dur + 0.1);

});

}


// ── sharp impact stab ──

function stab(t) {

if (!AC || muted) return;

// low hit

const o = AC.createOscillator(), g = AC.createGain();

o.type = ‘sawtooth’; o.frequency.value = 55;

g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.5, t);

g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.18);

o.connect(g); g.connect(MG); o.start(t); o.stop(t + 0.2);

// noise burst

const sr = AC.sampleRate;

const buf = AC.createBuffer(1, sr * 0.12, sr);

const d = buf.getChannelData(0);

for (let i = 0; i < d.length; i++) d[i] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * (1 - i / d.length);

const src = AC.createBufferSource(), ng = AC.createGain();

const hp = AC.createBiquadFilter();

hp.type = ‘highpass’; hp.frequency.value = 1500;

src.buffer = buf; src.connect(hp); hp.connect(ng); ng.connect(MG);

ng.gain.setValueAtTime(0.30, t);

ng.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.12);

src.start(t); src.stop(t + 0.14);

}


// ── eerie high tone (distant, floating) ──

function eerieNote(freq, t, dur, vol) {

if (!AC || muted) return;

const o = AC.createOscillator();

const g = AC.createGain();

const lp = AC.createBiquadFilter();

lp.type = ‘lowpass’; lp.frequency.value = 800;

o.type = ‘sine’; o.frequency.value = freq;

o.detune.value = 8;

o.connect(lp); lp.connect(g); g.connect(MG);

g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);

g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol || 0.08, t + 0.8);

g.gain.setValueAtTime(vol || 0.08, t + dur - 1.2);

g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + dur);

o.start(t); o.stop(t + dur + 0.1);

}


function playSuspense() {

if (!AC || played) return;

played = true;

const N = AC.currentTime + 0.2;

const s = n => N + n;


// ── 0s: IMMEDIATE IMPACT — starts right away, no silence

// Deep drone audible on all speakers

drone(82.4, s(0), 30, 0.22, 600); // E2 — clearly audible root

drone(55, s(0), 30, 0.14, 400); // A1 undertone

drone(110, s(0), 30, 0.08, 900); // E3 upper shimmer

rumble(s(0), 10, 280, 0.10); // low texture rumble


// ── 0-4s: SPARSE EARLY HITS

thud(s(0.5), 0.42);

thud(s(2.2), 0.38);

eerieNote(246.9, s(1), 5, 0.10); // B3 — eerie tone enters early


// ── 4-10s: HEARTBEAT ENTERS

[4, 5.5, 6.8, 8.0, 9.0].forEach((t, i) => thud(s(t), 0.36 + i * 0.02));

swell(110, s(5), 5, 0.07);

eerieNote(196, s(6), 5, 0.09);

rumble(s(5), 7, 320, 0.08);


// ── 10-16s: TENSION ACCELERATES

[10, 10.9, 11.7, 12.4, 13.0, 13.55, 14.05, 14.5, 14.9, 15.25].forEach((t, i) =>

thud(s(t), 0.33 + i * 0.015)

);

swell(138.6, s(11), 5, 0.08); // C#3 swell — chromatic, unsettling

eerieNote(329.6, s(12), 5, 0.10);

drone(164.8, s(10), 8, 0.10, 700);

rumble(s(11), 6, 400, 0.09);


// ── 16-18s: SILENCE BREAK — one beat of near-silence

// (just the root drone underneath)


// ── 18s: DOUBLE IMPACT STAB

stab(s(18));

stab(s(18.08));


// ── 18.5-25s: EERIE AFTERMATH

drone(82.4, s(18.5), 10, 0.12, 500);

eerieNote(220, s(19), 5, 0.09);

eerieNote(261.6, s(21), 5, 0.08);

eerieNote(196, s(23), 4, 0.07);

swell(82.4, s(20), 6, 0.06);

rumble(s(19), 8, 250, 0.07);

[19.5, 21.2, 22.8].forEach(t => thud(s(t), 0.22));


// ── 25-32s: FINAL FADE

drone(82.4, s(25), 9, 0.10, 450);

eerieNote(164.8, s(26), 5, 0.07);

rumble(s(26), 7, 200, 0.05);

[25.5, 27.5, 29.2].forEach(t => thud(s(t), 0.18));


const fadeAt = N + 28;

MG.gain.setValueAtTime(0.18, fadeAt);

MG.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, fadeAt + 5);

}


// ══════════════════════════════════════════════

// SCENE ENGINE

// ══════════════════════════════════════════════

const SCENES = [

{ id:‘sc1’, lbl:‘INCOMING TRANSMISSION’, dur:4500 },

{ id:‘sc2’, lbl:‘ALL ABOARD THE PARTY BUS’, dur:5000 },

{ id:‘sc3’, lbl:‘VICTORY ROYALE’, dur:5000 },

{ id:‘sc4’, lbl:‘MISSION OBJECTIVE’, dur:4500 },

{ id:‘sc5’, lbl:‘MISSION BRIEFING’, dur:8000 },

];

const TOTAL = SCENES.reduce((a,s) => a + s.dur, 0);


let elapsed=0, running=false, rafId=null, lastT=null, cur=-1;


const bgEl = document.getElementById(‘bg’);

const beamsEl = document.getElementById(‘beams’);

const progEl = document.getElementById(‘prog’);

const lblEl = document.getElementById(‘lbl’);

const playBtn = document.getElementById(‘playBtn’);

const ctrlEl = document.getElementById(‘ctrl’);

const flEl = document.getElementById(‘fl’);

const busWrap = document.getElementById(‘busWrap’);

const corners = [‘ctl’,‘ctr’,‘cbl’,‘cbr’].map(id => document.getElementById(id));


// Bus window disco

const WC = [

[‘rgba(0,212,255,.26)’,‘rgba(123,47,255,.26)’,‘rgba(255,0,102,.26)’,‘rgba(0,212,255,.26)’,‘rgba(255,149,0,.26)’],

[‘rgba(255,149,0,.26)’,‘rgba(0,212,255,.26)’,‘rgba(123,47,255,.26)’,‘rgba(255,0,102,.26)’,‘rgba(0,212,255,.26)’],

];

let wf = 0;

setInterval(() => {

if (!running) return;

wf = 1 - wf;

[‘bw1’,‘bw2’,‘bw3’,‘bw4’,‘bw5’].forEach((id, i) => {

const el = document.getElementById(id);

if (el) el.setAttribute(‘fill’, WC[wf][i]);

});

}, 480);


function doFlash(col) {

flEl.style.background = col || ‘rgba(0,212,255,.1)’;

flEl.style.opacity = ‘1’;

setTimeout(() => { flEl.style.transition = ‘opacity .7s’; flEl.style.opacity = ‘0’; }, 55);

setTimeout(() => { flEl.style.transition = ‘’; }, 800);

}


function showScene(id) {

SCENES.forEach(s => document.getElementById(s.id).classList.remove(‘show’));

if (!id) return;

setTimeout(() => document.getElementById(id)?.classList.add(‘show’), 220);

}


function runScene(idx) {

if (idx >= SCENES.length) { finish(); return; }

cur = idx;

const sc = SCENES[idx];

lblEl.style.opacity = ‘0’;

setTimeout(() => { lblEl.textContent = sc.lbl; lblEl.style.opacity = ‘1’; }, 300);


if (idx === 0) {

showScene(‘sc1’);

doFlash(‘rgba(0,212,255,.1)’);

busWrap.style.display = ‘none’;

}


if (idx === 1) {

showScene(‘sc2’);

doFlash(‘rgba(255,215,0,.08)’);

busWrap.style.display = ‘block’;

busWrap.classList.remove(‘drive’);

void busWrap.offsetWidth;

busWrap.classList.add(‘drive’);

}


if (idx === 2) {

showScene(‘sc3’);

doFlash(‘rgba(255,215,0,.15)’);

busWrap.style.display = ‘none’;

bgEl.style.background = ‘linear-gradient(180deg,#08060a 0%,#120a0a 50%,#1a0a00 100%)’;

corners.forEach(c => c.style.borderColor = ‘rgba(255,215,0,.45)’);

beamsEl.style.opacity = ‘0’;

}


if (idx === 3) {

showScene(‘sc4’);

doFlash(‘rgba(255,0,102,.15)’);

beamsEl.style.opacity = ‘1’;

bgEl.style.background = ‘linear-gradient(180deg,#060010 0%,#0e0020 50%,#160030 100%)’;

corners.forEach(c => c.style.borderColor = ‘rgba(255,0,102,.45)’);

busWrap.style.display = ‘none’;

}


if (idx === 4) {

showScene(‘sc5’);

doFlash(‘rgba(0,212,255,.1)’);

beamsEl.style.opacity = ‘0’;

bgEl.style.background = ‘’;

corners.forEach(c => c.style.borderColor = ‘rgba(0,212,255,.45)’);

busWrap.style.display = ‘none’;

}

}


function finish() {

running = false;

lblEl.textContent = ‘HAPPY BIRTHDAY ANAKIN — VICTORY ROYALE!’;

ctrlEl.textContent = ‘REPLAY’; ctrlEl.style.display = ‘block’;

playBtn.style.display = ‘none’;

}


function reset() {

cancelAnimationFrame(rafId);

running=false; elapsed=0; lastT=null; cur=-1; played=false;

SCENES.forEach(s => document.getElementById(s.id).classList.remove(‘show’));

beamsEl.style.opacity = ‘0’;

bgEl.style.background = ‘’;

progEl.style.width = ‘0%’;

lblEl.textContent = ‘Press play’;

corners.forEach(c => c.style.borderColor = ‘rgba(0,212,255,.45)’);

busWrap.classList.remove(‘drive’);

busWrap.style.display = ‘none’;


}


function go() {

if (running) return;

initCtx();

reset();

running = true;

playBtn.style.display = ‘none’;

ctrlEl.textContent = ‘SKIP’; ctrlEl.style.display = ‘block’;

setTimeout(() => { playSuspense(); rafId = requestAnimationFrame(tick); }, 200);

}


function skip() {

if (!running) { reset(); go(); return; }

const next = cur + 1;

if (next >= SCENES.length) { finish(); return; }

elapsed = SCENES.slice(0, next).reduce((a,s) => a + s.dur, 0);

runScene(next);

}


function tick(ts) {

if (!running) return;

if (!lastT) lastT = ts;

elapsed += ts - lastT; lastT = ts;

progEl.style.width = Math.min(elapsed / TOTAL * 100, 100) + ‘%’;

let sc = 0;

for (let i = 0; i < SCENES.length; i++) {

const se = sc + SCENES[i].dur;

if (elapsed >= sc && elapsed < se && cur < i) runScene(i);

sc = se;

}

if (elapsed >= TOTAL) { finish(); return; }

rafId = requestAnimationFrame(tick);

}

</script>


</body>

</html>
